if (!is_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_access')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: dev/generate_wellknown_other_access');
	writefile_7();
	if (!is_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_access')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): dev/generate_wellknown_other_access');
	} else if (sha1_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_access') != 'b1ae6d626a2aa6819aecd0e009602eeeab25cd76') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): dev/generate_wellknown_other_access');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('dev/generate_wellknown_other_access', 0755)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of dev/generate_wellknown_other_access');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_access') !== 'b1ae6d626a2aa6819aecd0e009602eeeab25cd76') {
		if (@sha1_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_access') !== 'fc6640358e6cba99a4f25c4a0621918d7d3a481a') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: dev/generate_wellknown_other_access');
			$tmp = pathinfo('dev/generate_wellknown_other_access');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('dev/generate_wellknown_other_access')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('dev/generate_wellknown_other_access', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_7();
		if (@sha1_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_access') !== 'b1ae6d626a2aa6819aecd0e009602eeeab25cd76') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): dev/generate_wellknown_other_access');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_firebird')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: dev/generate_wellknown_other_firebird');
	writefile_8();
	if (!is_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_firebird')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): dev/generate_wellknown_other_firebird');
	} else if (sha1_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_firebird') != '8919eedd814f47c0a1b10a30b008aab5ececae0d') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): dev/generate_wellknown_other_firebird');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('dev/generate_wellknown_other_firebird', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of dev/generate_wellknown_other_firebird');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_firebird') !== '8919eedd814f47c0a1b10a30b008aab5ececae0d') {
		if (@sha1_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_firebird') !== 'f20756e3c582c758204923893a6c0601661e672b') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: dev/generate_wellknown_other_firebird');
			$tmp = pathinfo('dev/generate_wellknown_other_firebird');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('dev/generate_wellknown_other_firebird')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('dev/generate_wellknown_other_firebird', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_8();
		if (@sha1_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_firebird') !== '8919eedd814f47c0a1b10a30b008aab5ececae0d') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): dev/generate_wellknown_other_firebird');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_mssql')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: dev/generate_wellknown_other_mssql');
	writefile_9();
	if (!is_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_mssql')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): dev/generate_wellknown_other_mssql');
	} else if (sha1_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_mssql') != '33e286d6aa3d4cb6a87380ec0318514dc283af94') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): dev/generate_wellknown_other_mssql');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('dev/generate_wellknown_other_mssql', 0755)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of dev/generate_wellknown_other_mssql');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_mssql') !== '33e286d6aa3d4cb6a87380ec0318514dc283af94') {
		if (@sha1_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_mssql') !== '8d5a984d3a905c7c4f6d2ee7c851ef8446e2c14a') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: dev/generate_wellknown_other_mssql');
			$tmp = pathinfo('dev/generate_wellknown_other_mssql');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('dev/generate_wellknown_other_mssql')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('dev/generate_wellknown_other_mssql', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_9();
		if (@sha1_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_mssql') !== '33e286d6aa3d4cb6a87380ec0318514dc283af94') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): dev/generate_wellknown_other_mssql');
		}
	}
}

// Files different: dev/generate_wellknown_other_mysql

if (!is_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_mysql')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: dev/generate_wellknown_other_mysql');
	writefile_10();
	if (!is_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_mysql')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): dev/generate_wellknown_other_mysql');
	} else if (sha1_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_mysql') != '9ec3d949fba0ecdcb7d4be9cbd454aed950f7078') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): dev/generate_wellknown_other_mysql');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('dev/generate_wellknown_other_mysql', 0755)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of dev/generate_wellknown_other_mysql');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_mysql') !== '9ec3d949fba0ecdcb7d4be9cbd454aed950f7078') {
		if (@sha1_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_mysql') !== 'a6b1cb1f82b95cea5cfc5aa17cc2ed6b8ed00398') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: dev/generate_wellknown_other_mysql');
			$tmp = pathinfo('dev/generate_wellknown_other_mysql');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('dev/generate_wellknown_other_mysql')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('dev/generate_wellknown_other_mysql', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_10();
		if (@sha1_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_mysql') !== '9ec3d949fba0ecdcb7d4be9cbd454aed950f7078') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): dev/generate_wellknown_other_mysql');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_oracle')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: dev/generate_wellknown_other_oracle');
	writefile_11();
	if (!is_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_oracle')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): dev/generate_wellknown_other_oracle');
	} else if (sha1_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_oracle') != '3d46b9d5b76a9d6b1149bc0bf1a81c5b50b47fd7') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): dev/generate_wellknown_other_oracle');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('dev/generate_wellknown_other_oracle', 0755)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of dev/generate_wellknown_other_oracle');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_oracle') !== '3d46b9d5b76a9d6b1149bc0bf1a81c5b50b47fd7') {
		if (@sha1_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_oracle') !== '132f278f213cad86aaefca20b734fec410175f9c') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: dev/generate_wellknown_other_oracle');
			$tmp = pathinfo('dev/generate_wellknown_other_oracle');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('dev/generate_wellknown_other_oracle')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('dev/generate_wellknown_other_oracle', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_11();
		if (@sha1_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_oracle') !== '3d46b9d5b76a9d6b1149bc0bf1a81c5b50b47fd7') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): dev/generate_wellknown_other_oracle');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_pgsql')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: dev/generate_wellknown_other_pgsql');
	writefile_12();
	if (!is_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_pgsql')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): dev/generate_wellknown_other_pgsql');
	} else if (sha1_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_pgsql') != '17c42af9dc69a7a9d219b5e24236e21d80036e82') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): dev/generate_wellknown_other_pgsql');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('dev/generate_wellknown_other_pgsql', 0755)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of dev/generate_wellknown_other_pgsql');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_pgsql') !== '17c42af9dc69a7a9d219b5e24236e21d80036e82') {
		if (@sha1_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_pgsql') !== '6976392dbc663c3569525ddb795c0794a0749e77') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: dev/generate_wellknown_other_pgsql');
			$tmp = pathinfo('dev/generate_wellknown_other_pgsql');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('dev/generate_wellknown_other_pgsql')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('dev/generate_wellknown_other_pgsql', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_12();
		if (@sha1_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_pgsql') !== '17c42af9dc69a7a9d219b5e24236e21d80036e82') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): dev/generate_wellknown_other_pgsql');
		}
	}
}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/mysql/sql/wellknown_other.sql');
	writefile_20();
	if (!is_file('plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/mysql/sql/wellknown_other.sql')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/mysql/sql/wellknown_other.sql');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/mysql/sql/wellknown_other.sql') != 'bbec0e1446970488a221d8ad2084cad5829d03e9') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/mysql/sql/wellknown_other.sql');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/mysql/sql/wellknown_other.sql', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/mysql/sql/wellknown_other.sql');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/mysql/sql/wellknown_other.sql') !== 'bbec0e1446970488a221d8ad2084cad5829d03e9') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/mysql/sql/wellknown_other.sql') !== '879ea03be12f77bc7ab0025b34cdf403820ad86a') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/mysql/sql/wellknown_other.sql');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/mysql/sql/wellknown_other.sql');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/mysql/sql/wellknown_other.sql')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/mysql/sql/wellknown_other.sql', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_20();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/mysql/sql/wellknown_other.sql') !== 'bbec0e1446970488a221d8ad2084cad5829d03e9') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/mysql/sql/wellknown_other.sql');
		}
	}
}

		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/installed.json');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('vendor/composer/installed.json', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of vendor/composer/installed.json');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.json') !== '083b476b9a0f70fef16a56638e8abec34db2ecfd') {
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.json') !== '15c8886444e3bb62e5bd3388a2f5b9f590317036') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: vendor/composer/installed.json');
			$tmp = pathinfo('vendor/composer/installed.json');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('vendor/composer/installed.json')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('vendor/composer/installed.json', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_24();
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.json') !== '083b476b9a0f70fef16a56638e8abec34db2ecfd') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/installed.json');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('vendor/composer/installed.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: vendor/composer/installed.php');
	writefile_25();
	if (!is_file('vendor/composer/installed.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): vendor/composer/installed.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.php') != '4a26e5e37b05edb00672846129c4800320990dc6') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/installed.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('vendor/composer/installed.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of vendor/composer/installed.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.php') !== '4a26e5e37b05edb00672846129c4800320990dc6') {
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.php') !== '1ec8a1d841a3914d332e005792cd3b41050d1a0e') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: vendor/composer/installed.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('vendor/composer/installed.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('vendor/composer/installed.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('vendor/composer/installed.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_25();
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.php') !== '4a26e5e37b05edb00672846129c4800320990dc6') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/installed.php');
		}
	}
}
